# Memory leak scan report

Date: 2026-07-21

Objective: Scan non-test, non-Rust files in the repository for potential memory-leak paths and capture per-file scan outcome.

Scope:
- Excluded tests/** and **/*.rs (Rust sources).
- Included all remaining tracked files, including build artifacts.
- Files classified as non-text/binary are listed separately and not pattern-scanned with source-level regex.

## Scan universe
- Total files scanned (listed): 8620
- Text files with memory-API pattern matches: 70
- Text files with no memory-API pattern matches: 650
- Non-text/binary files: 7900

## Method
- Built full non-test/non-Rust file universe using ripgrep.
- Classified each file by MIME type.
- On text-like files, one-pass rg search for memory API tokens:
  - malloc, calloc, realloc, strdup, free, mmap, munmap, asprintf, vasprintf, aligned_alloc, posix_memalign, memalign.
- Files with matches were reviewed at call-site level for obvious missing frees/ownership drops.

## Findings

### High-confidence leak candidate
- src/linux_abi/x86.c
  - build_stack() allocates gecopy with strdup when parsing HL_GUEST_ENV.
  - No matching free for gecopy is present before function return.
  - Reference behavior: src/linux_abi/elf.c performs free(gecopy) after tokenization.
